# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
If the coins are independent of one another: ^re4My4oO

p11 = p1q1        p21=p2q1
p12 = p1q2       p22=p2q2 ^1IwDNuBP

If you were unable to express P as a tensor product then
the events are not independent ^svP8ylDt

(You can however, find a linear sum of probability vector tensors that can act as independent bases) ^ph9tL7kt
